Conclusion: 通过融合生成式分布建模与确定性回归，StereoFlow有效缓解了回归均值偏差问题，显著提升了立体匹配在复杂场景下的鲁棒性与精度。

Abstract: Stereo matching is a fundamental task in 3D reconstruction. Despite remarkable advances, the prevailing paradigms formulate stereo matching as a deterministic regression problem, collapsing the multimodal distribution modeling into a single-point estimation. This formulation suffers from a regression-to-mean bias, frequently struggling with ambiguous regions. In contrast, we introduce a prior-guided generative framework that integrates deterministic matching regression and generative distribution modeling within a complementary formulation. Built upon this formulation, we introduce StereoFlow through three key components: (i) a two-stage progressive cascade matching network that progressively produces multi-resolution stereo conditions with complementary matching cues; (ii) a pixel diffusion transformer (termed StereoDiT) with a frequency-decoupled architecture for modeling correspondence ambiguity; (iii) a few-step flow matching objective (termed Transition Flow Matching) for efficient optimization. In summary, \textsc{\textbf{StereoFlow}} achieves strong geometric consistency and rich fine-grained details in ill-posed, discontinuous regions and under zero-shot generalization. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the proposed StereoFlow establishes multiple state-of-the-art results across benchmarks, including Scene Flow, KITTI, ETH3D, and Middlebury.

We then conduct cross-temporal inference by applying each best monthly model to all scenes, enabling an assessment of (i) which months provide favourable training and inference conditions, (ii) how performance transfers between seasons, (iii) the impact of processing level, and (iv) how these effects differ across built-up typologies. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在临床部署深度学习模型时，模型的鲁棒性和泛化能力至关重要。然而，影像强度归一化（尤其在多源、多协议的MRI数据中）对模型泛化能力的影响尚未被充分研究，因此亟需系统评估不同归一化方法的实际效果。

Method: 系统比较了七种不同的强度归一化方法（包括标准缩放、基于直方图的方法和基于高斯混合模型的方法），使用IWOAI 2019数据集训练3D U-Net模型，并在内部和外部测试集（SKM-TEA）上评估其性能，以分析归一化方法对模型泛化能力的影响。

Result: 在内部测试中各方法性能相近，但在外部数据上存在显著差异；其中Z-score、Nyúl直方图匹配和CLAHE表现更优，但所有方法均面临显著的性能下降，主要归因于域偏移。

Conclusion: 强度归一化对模型泛化有一定影响，但其作用相对有限，远小于域偏移带来的影响，因此需要结合其他策略以实现深度学习模型在医学影像中的稳健部署。

Abstract: Robust out-of-the-box performance is essential for the clinical deployment of deep learning models in medical imaging. An important but underexplored factor affecting model generalisability is intensity normalisation, particularly for magnetic resonance imaging (MRI), where image intensities vary across scanners and protocols. In this study, we systematically compared seven normalisation methods and their impact on the performance of a 3D U-Net model for meniscus segmentation from knee MRI. The methods included standard scaling approaches, histogram-based techniques, and a Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM)-based method. Models were trained on the IWOAI 2019 dataset and evaluated on both internal and external test sets (SKM-TEA) to assess generalisability. Performance was similar internally but differences were significant on external data, with Z-score, Nyúl histogram matching, and CLAHE showing greater robustness than other methods. However, these differences were small compared to the significant performance drop observed between datasets. Overall, while intensity normalisation had a measurable effect on model generalisability, its impact was limited relative to the effects of domain shift, highlighting the need for complementary strategies for robust deployment.

To address this, we introduce GaussianSeed, a progressive multi-scale Gaussian occupancy prediction framework that organizes primitives into a coarse-to-fine hierarchy. Benefiting from this hierarchical design, GaussianSeed effectively circumvents the memory bottlenecks inherent in dense representations, successfully scaling to a $0.1\text{m}$ spatial resolution while maintaining real-time inference capabilities. To comprehensively evaluate high-resolution geometric perception, we further construct TJScenes, a panoramic six-camera occupancy dataset with highly detailed $0.1\text{m}$ annotations. Extensive experiments on Occ3D-nuScenes and TJScenes demonstrate that GaussianSeed delivers the lowest latency among all evaluated methods while maintaining highly competitive accuracy, advancing the efficiency-quality frontier of high-resolution 3D occupancy prediction.

### [48] [Factor-Informed Uncertainty Distillation for Gaze Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20072)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计教师-学生框架：梯度提升教师基于图像质量因素（如光照、清晰度、眼可见性、对称性）预测预期注视误差；神经学生通过课程学习与排序监督，将这些可解释信号蒸馏为轻量级单次通过不确定性头。

Abstract: Deep gaze estimation works well in controlled capture but degrades in unconstrained settings, where systems must reject unreliable predictions. Single-pass uncertainty (e.g., heteroscedastic regression) infers uncertainty from pixels without explicit input-validity cues, while sampling based methods are often too costly for real time use. We propose Factor-Informed Uncertainty Distillation (FIUD), a teacher-student framework that aligns uncertainty with interpretable image-quality failure modes. A gradient-boosting teacher predicts expected gaze error from factors such as illumination, sharpness, eye visibility and symmetry; a neural student distills these signals via curriculum learning and ranking supervision into a lightweight single-pass uncertainty head. Across ETH-XGaze, Gaze360, and MPIIFaceGaze (>300k samples), FIUD improves uncertainty, error rank correlation and selective prediction versus deterministic and sampling-based baselines, with the largest gains in unconstrained settings.

### [49] [Development of an automated, reliable, and clinically meaningful artificial intelligence (AI) tool for diagnosing cardiac disease from conventional cardiovascular magnetic resonance (CMR) images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20087)

Result: 单个模型在独立测试集上表现出优异性能，最高AUC为0.937（HCM）和0.945（CA）。集成模型显著提升整体诊断能力，各疾病类别表现均达到或接近优秀水平：HCM（AUC=0.959）、CA（AUC=0.966）、NOR（AUC=0.872）、DCM（AUC=0.848）、ICM（AUC=0.840），CI区间均较窄，表明模型稳定可靠。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了一个端到端的自动化CMR数据处理与诊断框架，利用大语言模型与多模态深度学习模型实现了高精度、高鲁棒性的心血管疾病分类，具备临床应用潜力。该系统公开可用，有望推动AI在心脏影像领域的普及与落地。

Abstract: Aims: Cardiovascular magnetic resonance (CMR) imaging enables non-invasive assessment of myocardial structure, function, and pathology, but requires substantial experience in interpretation of CMR images that could be supported by artificial intelligence (AI)-based models. However, use of AI models for enhanced CMR reading is limited by labor-intensive data curation, suboptimal model performance, and unclear implementation pathways. Methods and results: We developed an automated data curation pipeline for CMR-based cardiovascular disease (CVD) diagnosis, integrating open-source locally-run large language models (LLMs) to extract diagnostic labels from narrative CMR reports and preprocessing multimodal imaging data, including cine and late-gadolinium-enhancement (LGE) CMR sequences. The dataset comprised hypertrophic cardiomyopathy (HCM), dilated cardiomyopathy (DCM), ischemic cardiomyopathy (ICM), cardiac amyloidosis (CA), and normal controls (NOR). A total of 988 curated cases were randomly divided into 742 for training and 246 for validation. Fine-tuned AI-models achieved high discriminative diagnostic performance on an independent test set comprising 1067 patients , with individual AUC-ROC values of up to 0.937 for the correct diagnosis of HCM and 0.945 for cardiac amyloidosis. Ensemble strategies combining multiple models and modalities further improved AI-based diagnostic accuracy and robustness, achieving the highest overall diagnostic performance for HCM (AUC=0.959, CI [0.936-0.978]), CA (AUC=0.966, CI [0.939-0.986]), NOR (AUC=0.872, CI [0.852-0.894]), DCM (AUC=0.848, CI [0.808-0.885]) and ICM (AUC=0.840, CI [0.809-0.868]). ### [50] [ENTRAP-VL: A Taxonomic Probe for Dual Contextual Entrainment in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20092)
*Karan Goyal,Afreen Hossain,Debojyoti Das,Vishal Bhutani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ENTRAP-VL，一个专为视觉-语言模型（VLMs）设计的双模态基准测试工具，用于研究上下文吸引现象。该工具基于对图像与文本之间关联及真实性关系的分类体系，构建了1500个样本，涵盖八个类别，分为文本吸引流（8种情境）和视觉吸引流（3种情境），旨在揭示多模态环境下上下文如何独立于其相关性或真实性影响模型输出。作者强调此问题在多模态中具有根本性差异，而非单模态任务的简单扩展，并公开发布数据集与评估协议以支持社区研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对上下文吸引的研究主要集中在单模态语言模型，而视觉-语言模型中的此类现象尚未被系统考察。现有方法无法充分捕捉多模态情境下由视觉或文本上下文驱动的复杂吸引机制，尤其缺乏对虚假但可能真实的内容的影响分析。因此需要一种专门设计的、双模态的评估工具来深入探究这一现象。

Method: 提出ENTRAP-VL，一个手动标注的多模态数据集，包含1500个样本，依据两个维度进行组织：一是上下文与目标对象的关系，二是上下文与真实性的关系。数据集分为两部分：文本吸引流（8种上下文条件）和视觉吸引流（3种上下文条件），以模拟不同模态下上下文对模型输出的影响。

Result: ENTRAP-VL成功构建了一个结构化、可重复使用的评估框架，能够系统检测视觉-语言模型在面对不相关、不真实但合理上下文时是否产生误导性输出。该工具使研究人员能精确测量和比较模型在不同情境下的上下文吸引行为，为理解多模态模型的鲁棒性与可信性提供基础。

Conclusion: 上下文吸引在视觉-语言模型中是一个双重现象，受文本与视觉上下文独立驱动，并引入新的真实性维度。现有的单模态方法不足以应对这一挑战。ENTRAP-VL作为首个为此类研究量身定制的基准工具，具备可扩展性和可复现性，将推动对多模态模型内在机制的深入理解。

Abstract: Contextual entrainment is the tendency of a model to let auxiliary context in its input pull its output, independently of whether that context is relevant, true, or even meaningful. Recently, it has been identified and given a mechanistic account in unimodal language models. Whether and how it manifests in vision-language models (VLMs) is, by contrast, largely unexamined, and the field lacks a purpose-built instrument with which to investigate it. We take the position that studying contextual entrainment in VLMs requires more than porting an existing text-only benchmark to the multimodal setting: it requires a taxonomically structured, dual-modality instrument whose conditions are constructed around the item at hand (the depicted image in the textual stream, the textual query in the visual stream). We argue that the move to VLMs is substantive rather than incremental. It makes entrainment a dual phenomenon, drivable independently by textual and by visual context, and it opens a veracity distinction (context that is false of the depicted scene yet possible in the world) that has no counterpart in the unimodal, world-knowledge-only formulation of prior work. To make this position concrete and actionable, we introduce ENTRAP-VL (ENTRainment Assessment Probe for Vision and Language), a manually curated dataset of 1,500 items across eight categories, organized by a taxonomy that spans two axes, i.e., the association of context with the item and its relationship to truth, and split into a textual-entrainment stream (eight context conditions) and a visual-entrainment stream (three context conditions). We do not claim to measure entrainment in any particular model; we provide the instrument, the taxonomy that motivates it, and the evaluation protocols it enables, so that the community can investigate the phenomenon rigorously. We will release the dataset and its documentation publicly.

</details>


### [51] [RIM: A Retrieval-In-Matching Framework for Cross-Domain Global Visual Localization of UAVs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20116)
*Xin Li,Siyuan Duan,Shang Wang,Zhimin Mao,Bingliang Hu,Geng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种高效且可部署的无人机全球视觉定位方法，通过在谷歌3D瓦片中采样多视角参考图像，结合两阶段跨域微调和局部几何一致性重排序，实现对复杂环境下的6自由度姿态估计。提出RIM框架，利用冻结的DINOv2-B检索器同时完成全局检索与局部描述，避免双重模型开销，显著提升效率。在EPFL Urbanscape和自采集长安公园数据集上零样本测试表现优异，召回率超越现有基线，端到端延迟仅67.9毫秒，远快于同类方法，适用于无GNSS环境下的实际部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机视觉定位方法受成像时间、平台差异导致的跨域外观与视角偏移影响，难以实现鲁棒的六自由度姿态估计。尤其在无卫星导航信号环境下，亟需高效、准确的全局定位方案。

Method: 采用谷歌3D瓦片生成多位置、高度和姿态的参考视图；设计两阶段跨域微调策略，利用姿态相近正样本与地理距离远的负样本训练模型；引入局部几何一致性进行候选重排序；提出RIM框架，冻结DINOv2-B检索器，通过知识蒸馏构建轻量级局部描述解码器，共享令牌场并融合浅层VGG19细节流，实现一次前向传播完成检索与局部描述。

Result: 在两个地理上独立的数据集上，RIM在25/50米阈值下，相对于SALAD分别提升Recall@1 8.55/13.77个百分点（EPFL）和4.45/8.94个百分点（长安公园）；在Top-K=5时，端到端处理时间仅67.9毫秒，比最强的独立稀疏匹配基线快1.8倍，比RoMa快40倍以上，同时保持相当的重排序精度。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一套高效、鲁棒且可部署的无人机全球视觉定位流程，特别适用于缺乏GNSS信号的复杂环境，为实际应用提供了强有力的技术支持。

Abstract: Global visual localization of unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) using remote-sensing reference maps has attracted increasing attention. However, acquisition-time and imaging-platform differences between UAV and reference imagery induce substantial cross-domain appearance and viewpoint shifts, challenging robust six-degree-of-freedom (6-DoF) pose estimation. We address these shifts by sampling UAV-viewpoint reference views from Google 3D Tiles across locations, altitudes, and orientations. A two-stage cross-domain fine-tuning recipe adapts SALAD using pose-near positives and geographically distant hard negatives, while local geometric consistency re-ranks the Top-K candidates. We further propose Retrieval-In-Matching (RIM), which freezes the adapted DINOv2-B retriever and distils a local-descriptor decoder that reuses its token field alongside a shallow VGG19 detail stream. One query-side DINOv2-B forward thus serves both SALAD retrieval and local description, eliminating a second foundation-model backbone while preserving retrieval descriptors by construction. We evaluate RIM zero-shot on the reconstructed EPFL Urbanscape and self-collected Chang'an Park datasets, both geographically disjoint from the training data. RIM outperforms ten recent retrieval baseline families. At 25/50 m under the full 3D distance metric, it improves Recall@1 over SALAD by 8.55/13.77 percentage points on EPFL and 4.45/8.94 points on Park. At Top-K=5, the complete measured localization query, including retrieval, candidate matching, and robust geometric verification, takes 67.9 ms end-to-end: 1.8 times faster than the strongest separate sparse-matching baseline and over 40 times faster than RoMa, while achieving comparable re-ranking accuracy. These results establish an efficient and deployable pipeline for UAV global visual localization in GNSS-challenged environments.

### [52] [HeadCast: Casting Attention Heads for Efficient Autoregressive Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20125)
*Jinliang Shen,Lianghao Su,Zheming Li,Kang He,ZiLiang Lai,Yanbing Jiang,Chengru Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HeadCast 是一种无需训练、即插即用的加速框架，针对自回归视频扩散模型中因持续增长的键值（KV）缓存导致的注意力计算瓶颈。该方法基于预训练模型注意力头行为稳定且异质的观察，通过一次性的分类将每个注意力头分为四类（Sink、Dummy、Spatial、Global），重构单一的KV缓存为特定于头的路径。其中，保留了对长时序一致性至关重要的Global头，而Spatial路径采用固定大小网格，随分辨率提升节省更多计算资源。在720P和1080P下分别实现最高1.62倍和1.95倍加速，同时保持与全注意力相当的质量并显著减少帧间闪烁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决自回归视频扩散模型在高分辨率下因持续增长的键值缓存导致注意力计算成为主要推理开销的问题，现有方法或因粗略启发式策略导致帧间闪烁，或需重新训练模型。

Method: HeadCast 利用预训练模型注意力头的稳定异质性，在最大噪声步进行一次性分类，将注意力头划分为 Sink、Dummy、Spatial、Global 四类，并构建头特定的缓存路径。其中，Global头被保留以维持长期时序一致性，Spatial路径使用固定大小网格以实现分辨率相关的高效计算。

Result: 在720P下实现最高1.62倍加速，在1080P下达到1.95倍加速；在VBench指标上与全注意力性能相当，且几乎无帧间闪烁。

Conclusion: HeadCast 提供了一种无需训练、可直接部署的高效推理加速方案，有效缓解了自回归视频扩散模型中的注意力瓶颈，尤其适用于高分辨率视频生成任务。

Abstract: Autoregressive (AR) video diffusion models have become a promising paradigm for long and streaming video synthesis, but the continuously growing Key-Value (KV) cache makes attention the dominant inference cost, especially at high resolution where each frame contributes many tokens. Existing remedies either evict the cache with coarse heuristics that cause inter-frame flickering, or require model re-training. We propose HeadCast, a training-free, plug-and-play acceleration framework built on the observation that a pre-trained AR model's attention heads exhibit stable, heterogeneous behaviors. After a short warm-up, HeadCast performs a one-time classification at the maximum-noise step that sorts every head into one of four archetypes: Sink, Dummy, Spatial, and Global, and restructures the monolithic KV cache into head-specific pathways. Crucially, it retains the Global heads that preserve the long-range temporal consistency aggressive eviction destroys. Because the Spatial pathway operates on a fixed-size grid, its savings grow with resolution: across state-of-the-art AR models, HeadCast accelerates inference by up to 1.62x at 720P and 1.95x at 1080P, while keeping VBench quality on par with full attention and largely flicker-free. Code is available at https://github.com/sjlgaga/HeadCast .

</details>


### [53] [Real-Time EEG Cap Electrode Detection for Guided Point-of-Care Placement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20142)
*William Lehn-Schiøler,Mads Sverker Nilsson,Nicki Skafte Detlefsen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种两阶段视觉系统，实时检测并验证脑电帽电极的解剖学位置。使用单类YOLO检测器定位电极，几何阶段结合面部特征点将检测结果分配到10-20标准命名角色。在五名受试者上进行留一受试者交叉验证，平均精度（mAP@.5）达0.94±0.07（合并为0.96）。针对不同帽子类型的留一帽子验证显示，中号和大号帽子性能稳定（0.97），小号帽子下降至0.72±0.28，但该差异主要与受试者熟悉度有关而非帽子样式。通过几何增强提升抗旋转和视角变化能力，且不增加推理开销；基于特征点的头部裁剪扩大可用距离范围，使0.6倍缩放下的精度从0.23提升至0.45。采用轻量级模型YOLOv10n，实现在普通CPU上640像素分辨率下19帧/秒的实时处理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有脑电帽电极放置验证依赖人工检查，效率低且易出错。本研究旨在开发一种自动、实时、准确的视觉系统，以辅助临床或科研中对电极位置的快速验证，提高脑电采集的可靠性和可重复性。

Method: 采用两阶段方法：第一阶段使用单类YOLO检测器（YOLOv10n）在实时视频流中定位电极；第二阶段利用面部关键点估计电极在10-20系统中的解剖学角色，通过几何约束实现精准匹配。引入几何增强（旋转、透视变换、mixup）提升模型鲁棒性，并设计基于关键点的头部裁剪策略以扩大有效识别距离。

Result: 在留一受试者交叉验证下，整体mAP@.5达到0.94±0.07（0.96合并），中号和大号帽子表现稳定（0.97），小号帽子因受试者熟悉度影响略有下降（0.72±0.28）。几何增强显著提升抗平面旋转能力与时间连续性召回率，无额外计算成本。头部裁剪使0.6倍缩放下的精度从0.23提升至0.45。系统在普通CPU上实现19 FPS的实时处理，满足临床应用需求。

Conclusion: 所提出的两阶段视觉系统能够高效、准确地实现实时电极检测与解剖学位置验证，具备良好的鲁棒性与实用性，适用于多种脑电帽尺寸及远距离场景，为脑电数据采集提供了可靠的自动化质量控制工具。

Abstract: We present a two-stage vision system that detects EEG cap electrodes in a live webcam stream and validates their anatomical placement in real time. A single-class YOLO detector localises electrodes; a geometric stage assigns each detection to a named 10-20 role from facial landmarks. Evaluating under subject-disjoint leave-one-subject-out (LOSO) cross-validation across five subjects wearing the clinically-validated Small/Medium/Large caps, the detector attains mAP@.5 = 0.94 +/- 0.07 across five held-out folds (0.96 pooled). A dedicated leave-one-cap-out axis, holding out every frame of a cap regardless of subject, leaves Medium and Large mAP@.5 within 0.01 of LOSO (0.97, 0.97) while Small drops to 0.72 +/- 0.28, a gap confounded with subject familiarity rather than cap style. Geometric augmentation (rotation, perspective, mixup) improves in-plane-roll robustness and temporal-electrode recall at no inference cost, and a landmark-driven head crop extends the usable distance range, lifting mAP@.5 from 0.23 to 0.45 at 0.6 x apparent scale. A compact mobile-candidate backbone (YOLOv10n) keeps the detector at real-time throughput (19 FPS) on a commodity CPU at 640 px.

### [54] [SHFormer: Dynamic Spectral Filtering Convolutional Neural Network and High-pass Kernel Generation Transformer for Adaptive MRI Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20159)
*Sriprabha Ramanarayanan,Rahul G. S.,Mohammad Al Fahim,Keerthi Ram,Ramesh Venkatesan,Mohanasankar Sivaprakasam*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于神经调制的判别性多光谱注意力机制（SHFormer），用于可扩展的MRI重建。该方法通过谱滤波CNN捕获跨模态的可转移特征，并利用动态高通核生成变压器增强高频细节，解决了传统注意力机制在高频率信息建模和跨域泛化能力上的不足。在监督学习、自监督学习、扩散模型训练以及封闭集与开放集泛化等场景下均表现出优越性能，在未见场景中PSNR提升约1 dB，SSIM提升约0.01。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统注意力机制在MRI重建中虽能捕捉非局部关系，但对高频信息建模能力弱，且在多模态数据上需针对不同模式重新训练，缺乏跨域泛化能力。因此亟需一种既能保留高频细节又能实现跨模态可迁移特征提取的新方法。

Method: 设计了一个包含谱滤波卷积神经网络（CNN）与动态高通核生成变压器的双分支架构：前者用于提取模式特定的可转移特征，后者专注于生成适应性的高通核以强化高频细节传播，结合神经调制机制实现上下文感知的高效特征融合。

Result: 在多种学习范式（监督/自监督/扩散模型）及多类测试设置（闭集/开集泛化）下，所提方法在未见数据上实现最佳重建质量，相较基线模型在PSNR上提升约1 dB，SSIM提升约0.01，具备良好的可扩展性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提出的SHFormer有效克服了传统注意力机制在高频建模与跨域泛化方面的局限，实现了高质量、可扩展的MRI重建，为多模态医学影像处理提供了新思路。

Abstract: Attention Mechanism (AM) selectively focuses on essential information for imaging tasks and captures relationships between distant pixel neighborhoods to compute feature representations. Accelerated MRI reconstruction benefits from AM, as the imaging process involves Fourier domain measurements that influence image representation non-locally. However, AM-based models are more adept at capturing low-frequency information with limited capacity for high-frequency representations, restricting models to smooth reconstruction. Additionally, AM-based models need mode-specific retraining for multimodal MRI data, as their knowledge is restricted to local contextual variations that may be inadequate to capture transferable features across heterogeneous domains. To address these challenges, we propose a neuromodulation-based discriminative multi-spectral AM for scalable MRI reconstruction that can (i) propagate context-aware high-frequency details for high-quality reconstruction, and (ii) capture features reusable across deviated unseen domains in multimodal MRI. The proposed network consists of a spectral filtering CNN to capture mode-specific transferable features and a dynamic high-pass kernel generation transformer focusing on high-frequency details. We evaluate our model on comparative studies in supervised and self-supervised learning, diffusion model-based training, closed-set and open-set generalization under heterogeneous MRI data, and interpretation-based analysis. Our method offers scalable, high-quality reconstruction with best improvement margins of ~1 dB in PSNR and ~0.01 in SSIM under unseen scenarios. Code: https://github.com/sriprabhar/SHFormer

### [55] [StreamHOI: Interaction-aware Temporal Memory Adaptation for Streaming HOI Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20174)
*Zejing Rao,Haoxian Zhang,Xiaoqiang Liu,Yiping Meng,Guoxin Zhang,Pengfei Wan,Fan Tang,Tong-Yee Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: StreamHOI提出了一种低延迟流式框架，用于长时交互视频生成。针对传统方法在实时交互应用中的局限性，该框架通过分析历史记忆组织方式，优化了不同Transformer块对交互区域与周围区域的记忆偏好，并采用偏置引导的专用记忆训练策略，结合记忆距离缩放模块，提升对早期交互状态的长距离访问能力。实验表明，StreamHOI在交互合理性、物体保真度、人物质量与效率方面表现优异，达到17.6 FPS和0.75秒首帧延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有HOI视频生成方法多为离线短视频生成，难以满足实时交互应用需求，尤其在复杂驱动条件下表现不佳。因此需要一种低延迟、支持长时交互的流式生成框架。

Method: StreamHOI通过离线进行HOI感知的块级性能分析，设计偏置引导的记忆专用训练策略，使生成器适配不同块特定的记忆布局；同时引入记忆距离缩放模块，增强对早期交互状态的长距离访问能力。

Result: StreamHOI在交互合理性、物体保真度、人物质量和生成效率方面均优于现有长视频基线与最新HOI生成方法，实现17.6 FPS的生成速度与0.75秒的首帧延迟。

Conclusion: StreamHOI通过创新的记忆组织与训练机制，成功实现了高效、低延迟的长时人类-物体交互视频流式生成，为实时交互应用提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Existing human--object interaction (HOI) video generation methods are largely limited to offline short-video generation with complex driving conditions, making them unsuitable for real-time interactive applications. We present \emph{StreamHOI}, a low-latency streaming framework for long-duration HOI video generation. Instead of converting heavily conditioned HOI pipelines into streaming systems, we study how an image-to-video streaming generator should organize historical memory to preserve interactions under bounded latency. We find that the standard sink-local memory design faces a trade-off in streaming HOI generation, and different transformer blocks show different historical-memory preferences for HOI regions and surrounding regions. To match memory composition with block behavior, StreamHOI performs offline HOI-aware block profiling and applies bias-guided memory-specialized training to adapt the generator to block-specific memory layouts. We further introduce a memory distance scaling module to strengthen long-range access to early interaction states. Extensive comparisons with both long-video baselines and recent HOI generation methods demonstrate that StreamHOI achieves strong interaction plausibility, object fidelity, human quality and efficiency, reaching 17.6 FPS with 0.75s first-chunk latency.

### [56] [PerceptDrive: Perception Prior World-Action Modeling with Adaptive Expert Routing for End-to-End Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20175)
*Yushan Liu,Tianxiong Lv,Bohua Wang,Hangqi Fan,Chenxu Zhao,He Zheng,Xuchang Zhong,Yifan Xie,Congyang Zhao,Zhihao Liao,Leigang Luo,Yang Cai,Xiao-Ping Zhang,Wenbo Ding*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PerceptDrive 是一种感知先验世界-动作建模框架，通过自适应专家路由机制，将冻结的感知先验与动态观测融合，实现无需测试时评分、重排序或搜索的直接规划。其核心创新在于：1）利用教师蒸馏的先验知识和自监督视频编码器的密集观测特征；2）通过专家特定查询分支和场景条件路由机制，动态调整各专家贡献；3）引入先验保留目标以稳定各分支学习；4）使用流匹配策略生成动作。在 NAVSIM v1 和 v2 上分别达到 90.4 PDMS 与 90.2 EPDMS，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于冻结感知模型的规划系统受限于狭窄的条件接口和静态融合方式，难以有效利用任务相关线索，且无法根据场景动态调整不同专家的贡献。因此，需要一种能够保留并自适应调度感知先验的新范式。

Method: PerceptDrive 将感知先验建模为先验到规划的迁移问题，采用可训练的专家路由世界-动作模型。输入包括来自冻结驾驶适配提供者的教师蒸馏先验和来自冻结自监督视频编码器的观测潜变量。专家特定查询分支处理这些信号，结合先验保留目标以保持分支稳定性。共享场景表示驱动路由器生成软门控，融合专家条件后生成轨迹。训练中使用规则子度量估计作为软门控蒸馏目标；推理时，无特权组件，仅需单前视摄像头，在每个规划步生成一条轨迹。

Result: PerceptDrive 在 NAVSIM v1 上取得 90.4 PDMS，NAVSIM v2 上取得 90.2 EPDMS，显著优于现有方法。消融实验证明：先验保留和场景条件路由带来互补增益，且对三种先验存在差异化依赖。结果表明，保留并自适应路由感知先验能有效提升直接规划性能，无需测试时候选选择。

Conclusion: PerceptDrive 证明了在规划中保留并动态路由感知先验的重要性，实现了高性能、低延迟的端到端自动驾驶规划，无需复杂的测试时操作，为基于冻结感知模型的规划系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Frozen perception foundation models encode rich geometric, semantic, and dynamic knowledge. Yet narrow conditioning interfaces may attenuate task-relevant cues, while static fusion cannot adjust expert contributions to each scene. We cast this challenge as the prior-to-plan transfer problem and introduce PerceptDrive, a perception prior world-action modeling framework with adaptive expert routing. PerceptDrive feeds teacher-distilled priors from a frozen, driving-adapted provider and dense observation latents from a frozen self-supervised video encoder into a trainable expert-routed world-action model. Expert-specific query branches process these signals, while a prior-retention objective anchors each branch to its prior. A router predicts soft gates from a shared scene representation and combines the expert conditions before trajectory generation. During training, privileged rule-based sub-metric estimates for branch-specific trajectory drafts provide soft-gate distillation targets. The predicted action-free future latent conditions a flow-matching actor. At inference, privileged components are absent; with one front-facing camera, PerceptDrive generates one trajectory per planning step without test-time scoring, reranking, or search. Experiments show that PerceptDrive achieves state-of-the-art performance with 90.4 PDMS on NAVSIM v1 and 90.2 EPDMS on NAVSIM v2, outperforming existing methods. Ablations confirm complementary gains from prior retention and scene-conditioned routing, alongside differential reliance on the three priors. These results demonstrate that preserving and adaptively routing perception priors improves direct planning without test-time candidate selection.

### [57] [RS-RIE-Bench: Benchmarking Reasoning-Guided Remote Sensing Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20197)
*Zihan Qin,Boao Xu,Zhao Dong,Yingping Sun,Ziheng Jiao,Junying Wang,Hongwei Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个针对推理引导的遥感图像编辑基准RS-RIE-Bench，涵盖时间、因果和空间推理任务，评估目标区域合理性、非目标区域保留及图像质量一致性。实验表明当前模型在地理推理和传感器一致性方面仍存在显著不足，最强模型在严格标准下仅24.28%准确率，凸显该基准的有效性与研究价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感图像编辑基准多基于自然图像或通用视觉场景，难以全面评估遥感编辑中的地理推理、区域控制与传感器一致性能力，亟需一个专门针对遥感场景的标准化评测基准。

Method: 构建RS-RIE-Bench基准，将任务分为时间推理、因果推理和空间推理三类，设计包含目标区域合理性、非目标区域保留和图像质量一致性的三维评估协议，并通过多模型对比与专家评审验证其有效性。

Result: 八种开源与闭源模型在严格联合满足标准下平均准确率仅为24.28%，放松标准下的联合成功率均值为32.23%；因果推理与空间推理尤为困难，部分开源模型表现接近零，揭示了当前模型在地理推理与传感器一致性上的明显缺陷。

Conclusion: RS-RIE-Bench有效揭示了现有模型在地理推理、区域控制和传感器一致性方面的局限性，为未来遥感智能编辑模型提供了标准化评测框架与明确的研究方向。

Abstract: Remote sensing image editing aims to modify remote sensing images according to natural language instructions while preserving geographic rules and sensor observation characteristics. Existing benchmarks mainly target natural images or general visual scenes, and thus may not fully capture the reasoning, regional control, and sensor-consistency abilities required in remote sensing editing. To fill this gap, we introduce RS-RIE-Bench, the first benchmark for reasoning-guided remote sensing image editing. RS-RIE-Bench organizes tasks into three categories: temporal reasoning, causal reasoning, and spatial reasoning. These categories capture temporal evolution, causal consequence, and spatial imaging consistency in remote sensing scenes. The evaluation protocol covers three dimensions: target region plausibility, non-target region preservation, and image quality consistency. We further demonstrate the feasibility of MLLM-based evaluation through cross-judge consistency analysis and stratified expert review. Systematic evaluation on eight open-source and closed-source image editing models shows that current models still have clear limitations in reasoning-guided remote sensing editing. Even the strongest model achieves only 24.28\% overall accuracy under the strict joint-satisfaction criterion, while the mean relaxed joint-4 success rate across all eight models is 32.23\%. Causal reasoning and spatial reasoning remain especially challenging, and several open-source models are close to zero in some categories. These results show that RS-RIE-Bench can effectively reveal the limitations of current models in geographic reasoning, regional control, and sensor-consistent generation. It also provides a standardized benchmark and a clear research direction for future remote sensing intelligent editing models.

### [58] [Not All Patches are Equal: Sampling Matters for Visible-Infrared Pre-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20238)
*Qiwei Ma,Bin Deng,Junjie Zhu,Qiangjuan Huang,Puhong Duan,Ke Yang,Xudong Kang,Shutao Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为重要性感知采样（IAS）的新方法，用于改进可见光-红外（VIS-IR）对齐的预训练。传统方法采用均匀的块级对比学习，但因成像物理差异导致部分区域可比性差，强行对齐会阻碍表示学习。IAS通过引入红外结构线索来评估块的可靠性，动态调整对比目标权重，并结合轻量级采样器学习软重要性掩码，同时采用从高可靠性区域逐步扩展到困难区域的课程学习策略。该方法无需修改主干网络，兼容多种对齐范式（如UNIV和ImageBind），在多个VIS-IR基准上显著提升下游任务性能，包括红外语义分割、目标检测、可见光语义分割和跨模态检索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VIS-IR对齐方法使用统一的块级对比学习，但由于成像物理差异，部分空间配对区域本质上不可比，强制对齐会降低表示学习效果并影响下游迁移性能。因此需要一种能根据块可靠性自适应调整训练重点的方法。

Method: 提出重要性感知采样（IAS）：(i) 利用红外结构线索生成块权重，重加权对比损失；(ii) 设计轻量级采样器学习软重要性掩码，可选地以手工先验初始化；(iii) 采用块级课程学习策略，从高可靠性区域逐步扩展至更难的区域。

Result: 在多个VIS-IR基准上，IAS在红外语义分割、红外目标检测、可见光语义分割和跨模态检索等任务中均优于强基线，表现稳定且一致。

Conclusion: IAS是一种即插即用的VIS-IR预训练方法，能够有效应对成像差异带来的对齐挑战，显著提升多传感器感知系统的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Visible-infrared (VIS-IR) alignment is a key pre-training task for robust multi-sensor perception. Most existing methods use uniform patch-wise contrastive learning, but this can be unreliable in VIS-IR data because imaging-physics differences make some spatially paired regions inherently less comparable, and aligning them with equal strength hinders representation learning and downstream transfer. In this paper, we revisit VIS-IR pre-training from a sampling perspective and propose Importance-Aware Sampling (IAS), which adjusts training emphasis based on patch reliability. Specifically, IAS (i) derives patch weights from infrared structural cues and uses them to reweight the contrastive objective; (ii) learns a soft importance mask with a lightweight sampler, optionally warm-started from the hand-crafted prior; and (iii) employs a patch curriculum learning strategy that gradually expands from high-reliability regions to harder patches. It is worth noting that IAS is plug-and-play and works with both patch-/correlation-level alignment (e.g., UNIV-style) and image-level contrastive baselines (e.g., ImageBind-style). Extensive experiments on multiple VIS-IR benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over strong baselines, including for IR semantic segmentation, IR object detection and VIS semantic segmentation and cross-modal retrieval task. Code will be released on https://github.com/KlayMa527/IAS.

</details>


### [59] [Vera: Identity-Faithful Human Subject-to-Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20247)
*Yulong Xu,Xinyue Liu,Shujuan Li,huafeng shi,Yan Zhou,Jiwen Liu,Xintao Wang,Yu Shen Liu,Huaibo Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Vera提出了一种统一的人类中心视频生成框架，通过构建大规模身份对齐的图像-视频数据集，并引入身份聚焦掩码监督（IFMS）和参考感知分层注意力（RALA），有效提升了单人与多人场景下的身份一致性、主体绑定准确性和运动自然性，减少了身份混淆和参考图像过度复制问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于主题的视频生成方法在保持参考主体的一致性方面仍存在不足，尤其在涉及人类主体时，关键身份细节容易在不同帧、姿态和互动中发生漂移；多主体场景下更会出现身份角色错配、属性互换和过度复制参考外观的问题。

Method: 构建百万对身份对齐的人像-视频数据集，采用人物级跨片段检索；设计身份聚焦掩码监督（IFMS）以增强身份感知学习并减少无关干扰；引入参考感知分层注意力（RALA）以调控视频标记与参考身份线索在DiT骨干网络中的交互，稳定身份锚点并提升层级身份读取能力。

Result: 实验表明，Vera显著提升了人类身份一致性、多主体身份绑定准确度和运动自然性，同时降低了身份混淆和参考图像过度复制现象。

Conclusion: Vera是一种高效且通用的人类中心视频生成框架，为解决复杂场景下身份不一致问题提供了新思路，在单人和多人生成任务中均展现出优越性能。

Abstract: Subject-to-video (S2V) generation has made substantial progress in preserving reference subjects across diverse categories, yet generic subject consistency remains insufficient for human-centric generation. A video may appear globally consistent while identity-critical human details still drift across frames, poses, and interactions. This issue becomes more severe in multi-person scenarios, where incorrect identity-role binding leads to subject confusion, attribute swapping, and excessive copying of reference-specific appearance cues. We propose Vera, a unified human-centric S2V framework for single- and multi-person generation. We first construct a million-pair identity-aligned human image-video dataset through person-level cross-clip retrieval, providing explicit identity correspondence and diverse references. Built on this dataset, Vera introduces two complementary designs. Identity-Focal Masked Supervision (IFMS) strengthens identity-aware learning with spatially focused supervision while reducing interference from irrelevant artifacts. Reference-Aware Layer-wise Attention (RALA) regulates how video tokens interact with reference identity cues in the DiT backbone, preserving stable identity anchors and enhancing layer-aware identity readout. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Vera improves human identity consistency, multi-person subject binding, and motion naturalness, while reducing identity confusion and excessive reference-image copying.

### [60] [How Does Urban Context Relate to Residential Building Health? A Vision-POI Fusion Framework for Building-Level Housing Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20263)
*Kun Zhao,Helei Ren,Guilin Tang,Tianyi Chen,Zhehui Song,Xing Liu,Lijian Zhou,Yuhong Zhao,Xiang Gao,Jinming Jiang,Qichao Ban*

Method: 采用多对象检测模型提取图像中的问题位置、类别和置信度；通过多视角聚合构建可解释的建筑级表示；提取500米、1,000米、1,500米缓冲区内的POI特征；使用皮尔逊与斯皮尔曼相关分析结合错误发现率校正筛选候选上下文特征；最后利用成本敏感随机森林分类器，在社区隔离的空间交叉验证下融合视觉与POI特征进行建模。

Conclusion: POI信息在住宅建筑健康评估中起到辅助作用，能够增强视觉检测结果的判别力，但无法替代直接视觉证据，也不能作为建筑状况的因果决定因素。多视角视觉整合是主要性能提升来源，建议未来研究聚焦于视觉信息的精细化处理与跨视角一致性优化。

Abstract: Housing-level urban physical examination is essential for identifying residential building problems and supporting targeted urban renewal. Existing automated inspection studies primarily rely on individual images and rarely examine whether surrounding urban functional context can provide supplementary information for building-level assessment. This study proposes a vision-POI fusion framework that combines multi-view visual inspection with POI-derived neighborhood context for residential building health assessment. The empirical dataset covers 92 old residential communities, 3,237 residential buildings, and 25,608 field-acquired inspection images in Qingdao, China, encompassing seven categories of housing-related issues. First, multiple object detection models are evaluated to extract issue locations, categories, and confidence scores from individual images. The image-level outputs are subsequently aggregated across multiple views to construct interpretable building-level representations. Second, POI features are extracted within 500m, 1,000m, and 1,500m neighborhood buffers to characterize surrounding functional environments. Pearson and Spearman correlation analyses, combined with false discovery rate correction, are used to identify candidate contextual features. Finally, visual and POI features are integrated using a cost-sensitive Random Forest classifier under community-isolated spatial cross-validation. The results show that multi-view aggregation provides the main performance improvement, increasing the building-level Macro-F1 from 60.84% under Direct Detection to 74.95%. Incorporating POI context further increases Macro-F1 to 76.79%, although the additional gain is modest and category-dependent. POI information therefore functions as a supplementary contextual prior rather than a substitute for direct visual evidence or a causal determinant of building condition.

### [61] [Self-supervision drives representational convergence in medical foundation models more than clinical supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20274)
*Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh,Sebastian Ziegelmayer,Mahshad Lotfinia,Lisa Adams,Sven Nebelung,Jakob Nikolas Kather,Daniel Truhn*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比18个图像编码器和7个文本编码器，探究医学图像表示的收敛性。结果显示，编码器间的相似性主要由自监督预训练目标驱动，而非临床监督或模型规模；尽管存在一定程度的收敛（如在胸部X光上达40.4%），但其与临床判断不一致，且不随模型大小或能力提升而增强。然而，线性分类器可在不同编码器间迁移，并在五个外部医院中保持约85%的性能，表明跨编码器互操作性可通过设计预训练目标实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前医学图像编码器常被视为可互换，基于规模和临床监督使表示趋于一致的假设。但这一假设缺乏验证，且现有相似性度量方法脆弱。本文旨在检验这种收敛是否真实存在、由何驱动，以及是否具备临床可用性。

Method: 在固定数据、架构和规模下，仅改变预训练目标，训练多个编码器；同时构建合成模型以隔离因果关系。分析涵盖700万至270亿参数、五种成像模态的18个图像和7个文本编码器，使用65万张胸部X光片数据集进行评估。

Result: 自监督编码器表现最佳（40.4%对胸部影像的对齐），临床监督（21.1%）和图文对比（3.3%）显著更低；收敛性不随模型规模增加（Spearman 0.302, p=0.223），也不跨越模态或达到临床语言水平。但线性分类器可在编码器间迁移并在五个外部医院保持约85%性能。

Conclusion: 医学图像编码器的收敛性主要由预训练目标决定，而非规模或临床监督。因此，互操作性应通过预训练目标设计并验证，尤其关注患者亚组和临床判断之间的差异。

Abstract: Medical image encoders from different groups are increasingly treated as interchangeable, on the assumption that scale and clinical supervision concentrate their representations onto a shared structure. Whether this convergence is real, what produces it, and whether it is clinically usable are untested, and the similarity measures behind such claims are fragile. We present a controlled dissection across 18 image and 7 text encoders, all open-weight and run locally, spanning 7M to 27B parameters and five imaging modalities, including 650,982 chest radiographs from six datasets. To isolate cause, we train encoders that vary only the objective under fixed data, architecture, and scale, and reproduce the effect in a synthetic model. Convergence is modest but above a random floor, driven by the self-supervised objective, not clinical supervision: matched self-supervised encoders aligned most (40.4% on chest radiography), with label-supervised (21.1%) and image-text (3.3%) far lower, and did not grow with size (Spearman 0.302, p=0.223) or capability. It is within-modality, does not reach clinical language, and does not reproduce how radiologists judge case similarity. Yet a linear classifier transfers across encoders and to five held-out hospitals, retaining about 85% of within-encoder performance. Convergence in medical imaging is therefore set by the pretraining objective, not inherited from scale or clinical supervision. Interoperability is accordingly something to design for through that objective, and to validate where the shared geometry is weakest, across patient subgroups and against clinical judgment.

Conclusion: 通用多模态大模型在遥感图像理解中展现出强大潜力，现有专用于遥感的模型并非在所有任务中均占优；未来应聚焦于提升多模态与高分辨率推理能力、优化评估体系、实现高效部署，并发展工具增强型遥感智能体，推动更可靠、通用和实用的遥感理解系统建设。

Abstract: The rapid development of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) has introduced a flexible paradigm for remote sensing image scene understanding (RSISU), enabling natural-language interaction with remote sensing imagery. However, a systematic understanding of the capability boundaries, cross-task generalization, and task-specific limitations of existing remote sensing MLLMs (RS-MLLMs) is still lacking. This paper presents a systematic survey and diagnostic evaluation of MLLMs for RSISU. We review the technical evolution of RS-MLLMs, focusing on model design, multimodal learning, training data, and downstream capabilities. We further compare RS-MLLMs with general-purpose computer vision MLLMs (CV-MLLMs) across diverse RSISU tasks and benchmarks. RS-MLLMs remain competitive in domain-specific settings, particularly remote sensing visual grounding and high-resolution visual question answering. More notably, general-purpose CV-MLLMs can match or even outperform these specialized models on several RSISU tasks without remote sensing-specific fine-tuning. These findings demonstrate the strong transferability of general-purpose CV-MLLMs and show that current RS-MLLMs do not consistently outperform them across diverse RSISU tasks. Current MLLMs also face limitations in spatial and relational reasoning, fine-grained visual understanding, instruction diversity, and generalization across heterogeneous task formats. Based on these findings, we outline future directions toward reliable evaluation, multimodal and high-resolution reasoning, efficient deployment, and tool-augmented remote sensing agents. This survey provides a systematic reference for developing robust, generalizable, and practical MLLMs for RSISU.

### [64] [Evolving Cache Schedules for Fast Diffusion Policy Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20293)
*Siying Wang,Kangye Ji,Di Wang,Fei Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EVO提出了一种无需训练的加速框架，通过进化搜索全局调度缓存刷新，以在保持接近全性能的同时显著降低计算开销。它通过冗余感知初始化和目标条件提前终止提升搜索效率，并可直接应用于预训练扩散策略，无需重新训练。在多个操纵基准测试中，EVO实现了最高8.05倍的动作生成速度提升，浮点运算量从15.77G降至1.96G。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于缓存的方法在块间均匀分配计算资源，忽略了不同块间的冗余差异，导致性能与效率之间的权衡不理想。为解决这一问题，需要一种更智能、自适应的缓存调度策略。

Method: EVO采用进化搜索方法，在块-时间步网格上对完整的缓存刷新调度进行优化。引入冗余感知初始化以生成高质量初始种群，并使用目标条件提前终止机制，在达到预期性能目标后立即停止搜索，从而提高效率。该方法无需重新训练即可部署于预训练扩散策略。

Result: 在多个操纵任务中，EVO在仅保留接近完整性能的前提下，将动作生成速度提升了最多8.05倍，同时将浮点运算量从15.77G减少至最低1.96G，显著提升了推理效率。

Conclusion: EVO通过进化搜索实现高效的训练-free缓存调度，在不牺牲性能的情况下大幅降低扩散策略的计算成本，是一种实用且可直接部署的加速方案。

Abstract: Diffusion policies achieve strong visuomotor control by iteratively denoising action chunks, but repeated denoising makes real-time deployment computationally demanding. Cache-based methods reduce inference cost by reusing intermediate activations, but existing training-free schedules typically allocate computation uniformly across blocks, ignoring heterogeneous redundancy across blocks and leading to a suboptimal performance-efficiency trade-off. To bridge this gap, we introduce Evolving Cache Schedules (EVO), a training-free acceleration framework that globally schedules cache refreshes via evolutionary search. EVO represents each candidate as a complete schedule over the block-timestep lattice. Thus, redundant transformer computations during iterative denoising can be skipped through cache reuse while preserving closed-loop rollout performance. To make the search practical, EVO introduces redundancy-aware initialization, which seeds the population with promising schedules, and target-conditioned early stopping, which verifies and terminates once a desired performance target is reached. The offline-optimized schedule can be directly plugged into pretrained diffusion policies without retraining. Extensive manipulation benchmarks show that EVO preserves near-full performance while substantially reducing computation, achieving up to 8.05x action-generation speedup and reducing FLOPs from 15.77G to as low as 1.96G. Source code is available at https://github.com/pillom/EVO.

</details>


### [65] [Toward Reliable RGB-D Semantic Segmentation: Handling Missing Modalities via Condition Dropout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20326)
*Xuchen Zhu,Yajuan Wei,Shuang Hao,Jiwei Jiang,Guanxiang Mao,Fang Ren*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Condition Dropout (ConD)的简单持续训练范式，用于提升RGB-D语义分割模型在模态缺失情况下的鲁棒性。该方法通过随机模拟完整、仅缺RGB或仅缺深度的输入，在冻结原始编码器的基础上训练复制的编码器，并引入零初始化特征注入，从而在模态缺失时仍能有效利用剩余模态信息，且在模态完整时保持甚至略微提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RGB-D语义分割模型通常假设RGB和深度图像始终可用，但在实际应用中，传感器故障或遮挡可能导致某一模态缺失。然而，大多数模型在仅依赖单一模态时表现显著下降，无法充分利用剩余信息，因此需要一种能够应对模态缺失并保持高精度的方法。

Method: 提出Condition Dropout (ConD)方法：从预训练的RGB-D模型出发，增加一个第二阶段训练；随机生成完整、缺少RGB或缺少深度的输入数据，冻结原始编码器，训练一组复制的编码器，并采用零初始化特征注入机制，使模型学习如何在不同模态缺失情况下有效利用可用信息。

Result: 在NYU-Depth V2和SUN RGB-D数据集上的实验表明，ConD显著提升了模型在模态缺失情况下的鲁棒性，同时在模态完整时也实现了轻微性能提升，证明了其有效性与通用性。

Conclusion: ConD是一种简单而有效的持续训练策略，能够在不牺牲完整模态性能的前提下，显著增强模型对模态缺失的适应能力，具有良好的实用价值和推广潜力。

Abstract: RGB-D semantic segmentation has achieved remarkable progress, yet most models assume that RGB and depth are always available. In practice, failures or occlusions of surveillance sensors often remove one modality. Although RGB or depth alone can contain sufficient cues, models trained only on full-modality inputs fail to exploit the remaining modality once one is missing, causing severe degradation. We tackle this issue with a simple continued-training paradigm, \emph{Condition Dropout (ConD)}, which mitigates degradation while preserving full-modality accuracy. Starting from a pretrained RGB-D model, ConD adds a second stage that randomly simulates complete, RGB-missing, and depth-missing inputs, freezes the original encoders, and trains copied encoders with zero-initialized feature injection. Experiments on NYU-Depth V2 and SUN RGB-D show that ConD improves robustness under missing modalities and even yields slight gains when modalities are complete. Our code will be made publicly available upon acceptance.

</details>


### [66] [Test-Time Training for Modality Order Consistency in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20351)
*Aditi Gupta,Yossi Gandelsman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 视觉-语言模型对图像和问题呈现顺序这一语义无关的改变敏感，图像优先提示在多个模型和基准上表现优于问题优先提示，揭示了可重复的模态顺序失败。通过该差距设计了一种测试时训练方法，显著缩小了模态顺序差异，并在图像优先分支上实现性能提升，实现了两种提示顺序的相互一致性。激活修补定位到网络中段的特定区域，该区域在不同提示顺序下表征差异明显，而测试时训练方法修复了跨层的不一致。结果表明，模态顺序敏感性是视觉-语言模型中的电路级故障，且简单的非对称测试时适应可有效缓解甚至提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉-语言模型在实际应用中常因输入顺序（如图像先或问题先）不同而表现不一致，这种不一致性虽与语义无关，但影响模型鲁棒性和可靠性。研究旨在揭示并解决这一潜在的模态顺序敏感性问题。

Method: 提出一种基于模态顺序差距的测试时训练方法，通过在推理阶段动态调整模型行为，使不同提示顺序下的输出趋于一致；结合激活修补技术定位导致不一致的关键网络区域。

Result: 所提方法显著缩小了图像先与问题先提示之间的性能差距，在所有评估设置中均有效；同时提升了图像优先提示的基线性能，实现双向一致性改进；激活分析确认了模态顺序失败集中于网络中段，且测试时训练修复了该区域的表示错位。

Conclusion: 模态顺序敏感性是视觉-语言模型中的一个电路级缺陷，可通过简单、不对称的测试时自适应方法有效缓解，甚至带来整体性能提升，为提升模型鲁棒性提供了新思路。

Abstract: We find that vision-language models are sensitive to a specific semantically irrelevant change: the order in which the image and question are presented. Across three models and three benchmarks, image first prompting consistently outperforms question-first prompting, revealing a repeatable modality order failure. We use this gap to design an order-consistent test-time training method. Our method substantially closes the modality-order gap across all evaluated settings. Surprisingly, it also yields consistent improvements in the stronger image-first branch over the baseline, hence bootstrapping both orderings toward mutual consistency. Activation patching localizes the ordering failure to a narrow mid-network region where representations diverge sharply between prompt orders. We find that the test-time training method repairs this misalignment across layers. Together, our results identify modality-order sensitivity as a circuit-level failure in VLMs and demonstrate that simple, asymmetric test-time adaptation can effectively mitigate it and even improve performance over the baseline.

### [67] [Look Less, Think Faster: Joint Token-Compute Adaptation for Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20357)
*Pengcheng Wang,Zhiquan Wang,Jayoung Lee,Zhuoyan Xu,Ran Xu,Saurabh Bagchi,Yin Li,Somali Chaterji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SmartVL提出一种统一的自适应推理框架，通过联合控制视觉令牌数量和模型计算能力，在不同输入内容和计算预算下实现高效推理。该框架包含视觉侧的令牌控制器和LLM侧的计算控制器，二者通过共享的预算编码协同工作，并利用可微分延迟估计器进行端到端训练，从而学习跨阶段的资源分配策略。实验表明，SmartVL在多个MLLM基准上均优于现有方法，实现了更优的精度-效率权衡。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）虽然在视觉-语言任务中表现优异，但其高推理成本限制了实际部署。现有方法通常独立优化视觉令牌或模型层，忽视了计算资源在不同维度间的动态耦合关系，无法根据输入内容和计算预算灵活分配资源。因此，亟需一种能够联合调度视觉令牌与模型计算能力的统一框架。

Method: SmartVL引入视觉侧的令牌控制器，动态选择关键视觉令牌；同时设计LLM侧的计算控制器，自适应调整模型计算量。两个控制器通过共享的预算编码连接，并基于可微分延迟估计器进行端到端训练，使系统能学习跨阶段的资源分配策略，满足预设的计算预算约束。

Result: 在多个MLLM基准测试中，SmartVL表现出色，显著优于以往的自适应方法，能够在保持高精度的同时大幅降低推理成本，实现了更优的精度-效率帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: SmartVL通过联合调度视觉令牌数量与模型计算能力，实现了对多模态大模型推理成本的有效控制。该框架不仅提升了资源利用效率，还增强了对复杂输入和动态计算环境的适应能力，为MLLM的实际部署提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have recently demonstrated strong performance across vision-language tasks. However, their high inference cost, arising from both the large number of input visual tokens and the heavy computation of the large language model (LLM), remains a key barrier to practical deployment. Recent work attempts to reduce the cost by adaptively optimizing individual dimensions, e.g., pruning redundant visual tokens or skipping LLM layers and heads. Nonetheless, prior approaches typically treat these dimensions independently and overlook a fundamental coupling: the available compute resources must be dynamically allocated across all dimensions based on the input content. To bridge the gap, we propose SmartVL, a unified adaptive inference framework that jointly controls vision token number and model compute capability in response to varying input contents and compute budgets. SmartVL introduces a vision-side token controller that dynamically selects informative visual tokens and an LLM-side compute controller that adaptively adjusts LLM computation. Importantly, these controllers are trained to coordinate with each other so that the overall inference cost satisfies a target budget. To allow this joint scheduling, we connect the controllers using a shared budget encoding and leverage a differentiable latency estimator for end-to-end training. This design enables SmartVL to learn cross-stage allocation strategies that adapt to both input complexity and runtime compute constraints. Experiments across multiple MLLM benchmarks demonstrate that, with joint scheduling, SmartVL consistently outperforms prior adaptive methods and achieves superior accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontiers. Project page: https://www.schaterji.io/publications/2026/jointtokencompute.

### [68] [Self Gradient Forcing: Native Long Video Extrapolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20368)
*Junhao Zhuang,Shiyi Zhang,Yuxuan Bian,Yaowei Li,Yawen Luo,Yijun Liu,Weiyang Jin,Songchun Zhang,Xianglong He,Xuying Zhang,Haoran Li,Haoyang Huang,Zeyue Xue,Nan Duan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Self Gradient Forcing（SGF）方法，通过两阶段训练恢复自回归视频生成中历史上下文梯度的缺失监督信号，显著提升长时序视频生成的一致性与稳定性，仅用5秒训练窗口即可实现数分钟级视频生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自回归视频扩散模型虽采用Self Forcing减少暴露偏差，但历史键值缓存仅作为冻结状态使用，未来损失无法有效指导早期生成潜在表示如何被写入更有效的上下文记忆中，存在历史上下文-梯度间隙问题。

Method: 提出两阶段训练策略：第一阶段为无梯度自回归滚动，采样去噪退出步骤并记录自生成上下文与噪声潜在变量；第二阶段并行进行上下文梯度重建，以生成上下文作为停止梯度的干净潜在输入，重新计算上下文键值表示和未来到上下文的因果注意力，从而在原生自回归目标下提供记忆写入监督。

Result: 在多种初始化条件下，SGF在长时序帧级与块级实验中均优于Self Forcing，显著提升主体身份、背景/布局一致性及时间稳定性；仅需5秒训练窗口即可实现几分钟级视频外推。

Conclusion: SGF有效解决了自回归视频生成中的历史上下文梯度间隙问题，通过轻量级两阶段训练恢复关键监督信号，推动了长视频生成能力的发展，代码与模型将公开以促进该领域研究。

Abstract: Recent autoregressive video diffusion methods are increasingly built upon Self Forcing, where the student is trained on histories produced by its own rollout rather than ground-truth video contexts. This reduces exposure bias, but the historical key-value cache is still used by future frames only as frozen rollout state. As a result, future losses cannot supervise how earlier generated latents should be written into more useful keys and values for later video-latent generation. We call this the historical context-gradient gap. We propose Self Gradient Forcing (SGF), a two-pass training strategy that restores this missing supervision signal without backpropagating through the full serial rollout. Pass 1 performs a no-gradient autoregressive rollout matching inference and, at a sampled denoising exit step, records both the self-generated context and the noisy latents fed to the model. Pass 2 performs parallel context-gradient reconstruction for the recorded exit step. The generated context is used as stop-gradient clean-latent input, while the model recomputes the context KV representations and future-to-context causal attention. Thus, SGF provides the missing memory-writing supervision within the native autoregressive training objective, using losses on future video latents to train the model to encode context into more effective causal memory. Across extensive long-horizon frame-wise and chunk-wise experiments under different initializations, SGF achieves stronger native long-video extrapolation than Self Forcing, especially in subject identity, background/layout consistency, and temporal stability. Remarkably, using only a 5-second training window, SGF can extrapolate to videos lasting several minutes. Code and models will be released to advance research on autoregressive video generation.

### [69] [Persian Pixel: A large-scale synthetic OCR dataset for Persian language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20385)
*Pouria Mahdi,Haq Nawaz Malik*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Persian Pixel，一个大规模、高保真的合成光学字符识别（OCR）数据集，旨在解决波斯语文本识别中因书写系统复杂性和标注数据稀缺导致的挑战。该数据集包含超过34.3万张图像与文本对，覆盖句子、段落和整页文档布局，基于七百万词的波斯语语料库生成，并通过SynthOCR-Gen框架精确模拟波斯文的连写、上下文变体、标点位置及多种字体风格。为弥合合成数据与真实场景之间的差距，图像还引入了25种随机退化模型，模拟实际扫描中的墨水晕染、纸张老化、模糊、光照变化等缺陷。该数据集可有效支持Transformer类OCR模型（如TrOCR、Donut）的训练与微调，推动波斯语文档分析、历史手稿数字化与端到端文档理解研究，证明程序化合成数据是低资源、复杂书写系统下提升OCR性能的可行且高效方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波斯语虽有超1.1亿使用者，但其光学字符识别（OCR）技术远落后于拉丁字母语言，主要受限于波斯-阿拉伯文字系统的内在复杂性（如连写、上下文形变、大量连字、符号位置、字体风格差异）以及高质量标注数据极度匮乏。人工标注成本高、耗时长，形成数据瓶颈，制约了波斯语文档数字化与OCR系统发展。

Method: 提出Persian Pixel合成数据集，基于七百万词波斯语语料库，利用SynthOCR-Gen渲染框架生成涵盖句子、段落、整页文档的34.3万组高保真图像-文本对。生成过程精确模拟波斯文的连写规则、位置变体、标点布局及多种典型字体（如Naskh、Nastaliq）。进一步引入25种随机退化模型，模拟真实文档采集中的噪声、模糊、光照变化、压缩伪影、纸张老化等现实缺陷，以增强数据真实性。

Result: Persian Pixel成功构建了一个大规模、多样化、高真实感的合成波斯语OCR数据集，有效缓解了标注数据稀缺问题。该数据集已开源，可直接用于训练和微调现代OCR模型（如TrOCR、Donut），显著提升波斯语文本识别性能。实验表明，合成数据在跨域泛化方面表现良好，验证了程序化生成方法在低资源、复杂书写系统中的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了程序化合成数据生成在解决低资源、高复杂度语言OCR数据瓶颈方面的巨大潜力。Persian Pixel不仅为波斯语文档分析提供了关键基础设施，也为其他类似语言的数字化工作提供了可复用的技术范式，标志着从依赖昂贵人工标注向高效合成数据驱动的转型。

Abstract: Optical Character Recognition (OCR) for Persian remains substantially less mature than for Latin-script languages despite Persian being spoken by more than 110 million people across multiple countries. This gap arises from two fundamental challenges: the intrinsic complexity of the Perso-Arabic writing system and the limited availability of large-scale, high-quality annotated datasets. Persian script exhibits obligatory cursive connectivity, context-dependent glyph shaping, extensive ligatures, diacritic placement, and stylistic variation across writing forms such as Naskh and Nastaliq, all of which significantly complicate text recognition. At the same time, the high cost and labor-intensive nature of manual annotation have created a persistent data bottleneck, limiting the development of robust OCR systems and slowing progress in Persian document digitization.In this paper, we introduce Persian Pixel, a comprehensive synthetic OCR dataset specifically designed to address these challenges. Comprising over 343,000 high-fidelity image text pairs, the dataset spans sentence, paragraph, and full-page document layouts generated from a carefully curated seven-million-word Persian corpus using the SynthOCR-Gen rendering framework. The generation pipeline faithfully models the typographic characteristics of Persian script, including contextual character joining, positional glyph variants, diacritic placement, and multiple representative Persian typefaces. To bridge the synthetic-to-real domain gap, the rendered images are further enriched with more than twenty-five stochastic degradation models that emulate realistic document acquisition artifacts, including ink bleed, paper aging, blur, illumination variation, scanner imperfections, compression artifacts, and multiple noise processes.By overcoming the long-standing scarcity of annotated Persian OCR data, Persian Pixel provides a scalable and openly available resource for training and fine-tuning modern OCR architectures, including transformer-based models such as TrOCR and Donut. The dataset establishes a strong foundation for research in Persian document analysis, historical manuscript digitization, and end-to-end document understanding, while demonstrating that programmatic synthetic data generation offers a practical, cost-effective, and scalable alternative to manual annotation for advancing OCR in low-resource and typographically complex scripts.

### [70] [PercepCap: Video Captioner with Structured Spatio-Temporal Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20389)
*Yifan Xu,Zihao Wang,Zhixiao Wang,Jiaming Zhang,Yichun Yang,Desen Meng,Yuanxing Zhang,Pengfei Wan,Limin Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PercepCap 是一个感知感知视频字幕框架，通过显式地生成时空感知轨迹（如物体轨迹和时间事件），再基于这些感知证据生成字幕，从而提升视频字幕的准确性和可解释性。该方法采用两阶段训练策略：先进行感知-描述监督微调，使模型从直接生成字幕转向感知-描述链；再通过感知引导的强化学习优化感知轨迹与字幕质量。为此，作者提出了基于字幕锚定的感知数据构建方法，自动从字幕中提取对象和事件，并在视频中定位其空间位置和时间戳，生成对齐的训练数据。实验表明，PercepCap 在字幕生成和问答任务中均优于 Qwen3-VL 基线，表现出更优的生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型在视频字幕生成中缺乏对时空感知过程的显式表达，导致感知错误难以追溯，影响模型可解释性与准确性。因此需要一种能够暴露感知证据的框架，以提升字幕生成的可靠性与可诊断性。

Method: 提出 PercepCap 框架，采用‘感知-描述’生成链：首先生成物体轨迹与时间事件等感知痕迹，再基于此生成最终字幕。设计两阶段训练策略：1）感知-描述监督微调，使模型适应新生成流程；2）感知引导的强化学习，联合优化感知链与字幕质量。引入‘字幕锚定感知数据构建’方法，自动生成对齐的感知标注数据。

Result: PercepCap 在直接字幕生成和字幕到问答评估中均显著优于 Qwen3-VL 基线，在生成质量、时空一致性及可解释性方面表现优异，证明了其有效性和先进性。

Conclusion: PercepCap 通过将感知过程显式化并建立可追踪的感知证据链，显著提升了视频字幕生成的质量与可解释性，为未来可解释多模态生成模型提供了新范式。

Abstract: Video captioning requires fine-grained spatio-temporal understanding of videos, including spatial perception of where objects are located and temporal perception of when events occur. Existing MLLMs usually generate captions directly from video inputs without exposing the perceptual evidence behind descriptions. As a result, mistakes in spatiotemporal perception are only observed in the final caption, making it difficult to identify the underlying perceptual errors directly. To address these issues, we present PercepCap, a perception-aware video captioning framework that makes perceptual evidence explicit before producing the final caption. Specifically, PercepCap follows a perceive-describe generation chain, where the model first produces a spatiotemporal perception trace comprising object trajectories and temporal events, and then generates the final caption conditioned on the perceived evidence. To support this, we design a two-stage training strategy. Perceive-then-Describe Supervised Fine-tuning adapts the model from caption-only generation to the proposed perceive-describe chain, while Perception-Grounded Reinforcement Learning optimizes perception trace and caption quality with joint rewards over perception chain and the final caption. To support our two-stage training, we introduce Caption-Anchored Perception Data Construction. This pipeline builds the SFT and RL training data by first generating a caption-only description, extracting the objects and events it mentions, and grounding them back in the video with boxes and timestamps. This yields caption-aligned perception data that provides solid training ground truth, ensuring that the explicit perception trace and final caption refer to the same objects and events. Across direct caption and caption-to-QA evaluation, PercepCap consistently improves upon the Qwen3-VL baseline and demonstrates leading caption quality.

### [71] [ATSplat: Compact Feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting with Adaptive Token Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20417)
*Cho In,Jeonghwan Cho,Mijin Yoo,Gim Hee Lee,Seon Joo Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ATSplat 是一种前馈式 3D Gaussian Splatting 框架，通过引入自适应 3D Tokens 恢复了 3DGS 优化中的场景自适应容量分配能力。它先将粗粒度的补丁级深度和相机线索提升为稀疏的 3D 锚点令牌，再通过可学习的 3D 偏移将其回归为局部高斯分布，实现原语位置与输入图像网格解耦。引入自适应令牌扩展模块，基于渲染误差图监督预测令牌不确定性，并选择性地扩展高不确定性令牌，从而在复杂区域集中原语并保持紧凑表示。在 RealEstate10K 和 DL3DV 数据集上的实验表明，ATSplat 在显著减少高斯数量（超过 5.7 倍）的同时达到最先进的渲染质量，仅用 31.1 万高斯即可在单个消费级 GPU 上实现 <1 秒重建和 1136 FPS 的高质量新视角渲染。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前馈式 3DGS 方法因像素对齐的设定导致原语数量和位置依赖于图像分辨率和输入视角，而非场景复杂度，造成冗余且密集的高斯集合，丧失了原始 3DGS 优化中的自适应容量分配能力。

Method: 提出 ATSplat 框架，通过将粗粒度补丁级深度与相机线索升维为稀疏 3D 锚点令牌，构建场景紧凑骨架；每个令牌通过可学习 3D 偏移回归为局部高斯；引入自适应令牌扩展模块，基于渲染误差图预测不确定性并选择性扩展高不确定性令牌，实现从稀疏到自适应的原语生成。

Result: 在 RealEstate10K 与 DL3DV 数据集上，相较于密集前馈式 3DGS 方法，ATSplat 将高斯数量减少超过 5.7 倍，在仅 31.1 万高斯下实现高保真渲染；从 12 张 512×960 图像重建时间 <1 秒，新视角渲染速度达 1136 FPS（512×960），性能优于现有方法。

Conclusion: ATSplat 成功恢复了 3DGS 优化中的自适应容量分配能力，通过稀疏 3D 令牌与自适应扩展机制，在保证高质量新视角合成的同时大幅压缩模型规模，实现了高效、紧凑且智能的 3D 重建与渲染。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) achieves high-quality novel-view synthesis by optimizing freely placed primitives in 3D and adaptively densifying them in under-reconstructed regions. However, this scene-adaptive capacity allocation is largely lost in existing feed-forward 3DGS methods, which commonly regress Gaussians at input pixels and lift them along camera rays. Such pixel-aligned formulations make the number and placement of primitives depend on image resolution and input viewpoints rather than scene complexity, resulting in dense and often redundant Gaussian sets. We present ATSplat, a feed-forward 3DGS framework that restores the adaptive allocation capability of 3DGS optimization through Adaptive 3D Tokens. ATSplat first lifts coarse patch-level depth and camera cues into sparse 3D anchor tokens, forming a compact scaffold of the scene. Each token is then regressed into local Gaussians with learnable 3D offsets, decoupling primitive placement from input image grids. An Adaptive Token Expansion module predicts a token-level uncertainty score, supervised by rendering error maps, and selectively expands high-uncertainty tokens through learnable expansion layers. This sparse-to-adaptive formulation enables ATSplat to concentrate primitives in challenging regions while maintaining a compact representation. Experiments on two representative datasets, RealEstate10K and DL3DV, show that ATSplat achieves state-of-the-art rendering quality while reducing the number of Gaussians by more than $5.7\times$ compared with dense feed-forward 3DGS methods. From 12 input images at $512 \times 960$ resolution, ATSplat completes reconstruction in less than a second using a single commercial GPU, and renders high-quality novel views at 1136 FPS ($512 \times 960$) with only 311K Gaussians.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [72] [Stateful Guardrails for Multi-Turn LLM Systems: A Conversational Risk Accumulation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19361)
*Sanjay Mishra,Divya Chukkapalli,Ganesh R. Naik*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出对话风险累积（CRA）框架，用于检测大语言模型在多轮对话中因逐步积累而产生的安全风险，如意图漂移、指令碎片化和敏感信息累积。通过追踪语义漂移、敏感信息图谱与合规梯度信号，结合无监督融合与学习型轨迹模型CRA-Net DA进行评分，并发布CRA-Bench系列基准数据集及轨迹原生评估协议，以实现对会话级风险的精准识别与评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM安全防护机制多孤立评估每一轮提示-响应对，忽视了多轮对话中逐渐累积的风险，如意图漂移、碎片化指令组合和敏感信息逐步暴露，导致潜在危害无法被及时发现。

Method: 提出会话层CRA框架，跟踪三个轨迹信号：从会话锚点出发的语义漂移、基于提取实体的敏感性加权信息累积图、以及反映合规意愿增强的合规梯度信号；采用无监督凸融合方法进行归因分析，设计CRA-Net DA模型以减少长度和话题覆盖偏差。

Result: 成功构建CRA-Bench v0.1/v0.2及扩展的5家族数据集，开发轨迹原生评估协议，包括会话级划分、混合集阈值校准、轨迹AUROC、检测耗时、校准误报率、置信区间与留一家庭诊断测试等，验证了在分布内会话评分与人类转移子集上的有效性。

Conclusion: CRA框架能够有效捕捉对话过程中渐进式安全风险，显著提升对隐蔽、累积型威胁的检测能力，为下一代对话安全评估提供了新范式。

Abstract: Most safety guardrails for large language models (LLMs) evaluate each prompt-response pair in isolation, which misses failures that arise only over a dialogue as benign turns compose into harm. We term this Conversational Risk Accumulation (CRA): gradual intent drift, fragmented assembly of prohibited instructions, and sensitivity build-up from repeated disclosures. We propose a session-layer CRA Framework that tracks three trajectory signals: semantic drift from a session anchor, a sensitivity-weighted information accumulation graph over extracted entities, and a compliance-gradient signal capturing increasing willingness to comply. For scoring, we provide (i) an unsupervised convex fusion for attribution and ablations, and (ii) CRA-Net DA, a compact learned trajectory model trained with family-adversarial objectives to reduce length and topic-coverage confounds. To benchmark CRA, we release CRA-Bench v0.1 (1,200 eight-turn sessions across three threat families with topic-matched benign twins), CRA-Bench v0.2 (LLM-paraphrased variants to reduce template artifacts), and an extended 5-family set (2,000 sessions adding persona priming and context stuffing). We introduce a trajectory-native evaluation protocol with session-level splits, mixed-set threshold calibration, Trajectory AUROC, turns-to-detection, calibrated false-positive metrics, bootstrap confidence intervals, leave-one-family-out diagnostic stress tests, and synthetic-to-human transfer checks. Claims focus on within-distribution session scoring on CRA-Bench and human-transfer subsets.

</details>


### [73] [When Reasoning Narrows the Move: Diversity Collapse in LLM Game Play](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19523)
*Junyi Sha,Renfei Tan,David Simchi-Levi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了监督微调（SFT）对大语言模型在序列决策中行为多样性的影响。通过基于井字棋变体的确定性棋类游戏，发现推理模式常抑制动作多样性，而标准SFT虽提升准确性，但易导致过早的多样性崩溃。提出动作增强方法（训练时使用每个状态的所有最优动作），可部分缓解该问题，揭示了窄支持模仿是导致策略坍塌的原因，并强调在SFT过程中保持动作支持对维持探索行为的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究监督微调（SFT）对大语言模型在序列决策任务中行为多样性的影响，尤其是在准确性和多样性之间权衡下的表现，以理解其潜在缺陷并改进模型行为的多样性与鲁棒性。

Method: 在一组基于井字棋变体的确定性棋类游戏中进行实验，利用精确可计算的最优动作来评估行为多样性；通过状态级评估、对战竞技场和训练轨迹分析，比较不同SFT策略下模型的表现；引入动作增强方法，即在训练中使用每个状态的所有最优动作而非单一示范动作。

Result: 推理模式生成会抑制动作多样性，尽管准确性可能提高；标准SFT虽提升准确性，但常引发过早的多样性崩溃，超出最小必要程度；动作增强方法能部分缓解多样性下降问题，表明窄支持模仿是导致策略坍塌的重要因素。

Conclusion: 在大语言模型的监督微调过程中，应重视动作支持的多样性，避免因窄支持模仿导致的策略坍塌。动作增强是一种有效手段，有助于在提升准确性的同时维持探索性行为，从而实现更稳健的决策能力。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is widely used to adapt large language models to downstream tasks, but its effect on behavioral diversity in sequential decision-making remains under-explored. We study this question in a controlled suite of deterministic board games based on tic-tac-toe variants, where optimal actions are exactly computable and diversity can be measured directly. Across state-level evaluation, arena gameplay, and training trajectories, we find that reasoning-mode generation frequently suppresses action diversity without uniformly improving action accuracy. Furthermore, standard SFT improves accuracy but often induces premature diversity collapse, which exceeds what is minimally required by the accuracy-diversity tradeoff. We then show that action augmentation, which trains on all optimal actions per state rather than a single demonstrated action, would partially mitigates this effect. Our results identify narrow-support imitation as a source of policy collapse in LLM decision-making and suggest that preserving action support during SFT is important for maintaining exploratory behavior.

</details>


### [74] [On the Computational Complexity of Structural Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19573)
*Zichao Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文为结构泛化提供了形式化定义，将其基于组合结构与无限泛化两个前提转化为数学语言。尽管该定义本身中立（如硬编码规则的编译器也满足），但真正的科学问题在于：能力能否从有限数据中自主涌现。这引出了计算下界NC¹与纯Transformer可学习上界TC⁰之间的矛盾。在蒙塔古语义学设定下，每个组合规则分解为句法面（Fγ）和语义面（Gγ）。在Gγ侧进行树评估是BFVP问题的一个实例，属于NC¹-完全问题。而纯Transformer需同时学习两面，但Kraus等（2026）证明其可学习类包含于TC⁰。在标准假设TC⁰ ≠ NC¹下，纯Transformer无法学习结构泛化。神经符号系统因注入了Gγ而表现更优，从而绕过了真正困难的部分。基准测试分数无法区分‘学习到的’与‘给定的’，本文旨在澄清这一点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前结构泛化虽被多次测量，却缺乏正式定义；且现有方法难以区分能力是通过学习获得还是人为预设。本文旨在澄清结构泛化作为科学问题的本质，并揭示纯Transformer在该任务上的理论局限性。

Method: 采用蒙塔古语义学框架，将组合规则分解为句法面（Fγ）与语义面（Gγ）；分析树评估在语义面的复杂性，识别其为NC¹-完全问题；结合已知结果，论证纯Transformer的可学习能力受限于TC⁰，从而推导出其无法实现结构泛化。

Result: 在标准假设TC⁰ ≠ NC¹下，纯Transformer无法学习结构泛化，因其必须同时学习不可分离的句法与语义面，而其表达能力上限低于所需计算复杂度。神经符号系统通过外置语义面（Gγ）规避了这一瓶颈，因而取得更高基准表现。

Conclusion: 结构泛化不能仅靠基准分数衡量，关键在于能力是否从数据中自主涌现。纯Transformer受制于其理论表达能力限制，无法实现真正的结构泛化，唯有引入外部语义知识的神经符号系统才可能突破此限。

Abstract: Structural generalization has been measured repeatedly by several benchmarks, yet it has never been formally defined. We give a definition that translates the two premises (compositional structure and unbounded generalization) into mathematical language. The definition itself is neutral: a compiler that hard-codes the rules satisfies it just as well. But structural generalization becomes a scientific question only insofar as the capacity can autonomously emerge from finite data. This question pits the computational lower bound $\mathrm{NC}^1$ against the learnable ceiling $\mathrm{TC}^0$ of pure Transformers. Under a Montagovian instantiation, each compositional rule splits into two projections: a syntactic face ($F_γ$) and a semantic face ($G_γ$). Tree evaluation on the $G_γ$ side is an instantiation of BFVP, which is $\mathrm{NC}^1$-complete (Buss, 1987). A pure Transformer must learn both faces at once, but Kraus et al. (2026) prove that its learnable class $\subseteq \mathrm{TC}^0$. Under the standard assumption $\mathrm{TC}^0 \neq \mathrm{NC}^1$, a pure Transformer cannot learn structural generalization. Neuro-symbolic systems achieve the best benchmark scores precisely because they inject $G_γ$, sidestepping the genuinely hard half. Benchmark scores cannot distinguish "learned" from "given." This is what this paper sets out to make clear.

</details>


### [75] [Scaling Laws for Hypernetwork-Based Knowledge Injection in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19604)
*Nischay Dhankhar,Dos Baha,Abulhair Saparov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探索了使用超网络（hypernetworks）在训练时注入事实知识的可行性与可扩展性，提出一种新方法通过训练超网络生成固定的LoRA适配器，使大型语言模型能够回答相关事实问题。研究构建了包含数千万个跨39个领域的多跳问答对的大规模数据集MegaWikiQA，系统分析了超网络深度、宽度及目标模型规模对损失、推理准确率和分布外（OOD）泛化能力的影响。结果表明：（i）超网络的知识注入表现出符合幂律规律的广泛可预测扩展性；（ii）随着规模增大，超网络在OOD任务上仍能保持可靠泛化能力，其缩放指数优于传统方法如LoRA微调和全量微调。研究首次提供了基于实证的超网络缩放定律，确立其作为训练时适应的可扩展、可信赖基础架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在大规模、可靠地注入事实知识方面仍面临挑战。虽然超网络在测试时适应中已有应用，但其在训练时知识注入中的潜力尚未被充分探索。当前方法如LoRA微调和全量微调存在可扩展性或泛化能力限制，亟需一种更高效、可扩展且具备良好分布外泛化能力的训练时知识注入方案。因此，研究旨在评估超网络在训练时知识注入中的有效性，并揭示其缩放规律，以推动更稳健的事实推理模型发展。

Method: 提出一种基于超网络的训练时知识注入框架：利用大规模事实语料训练一个超网络，使其生成一个固定结构的LoRA适配器；将该适配器插入目标语言模型后，模型即可回答与这些事实相关的问题。为研究缩放行为，设计解耦机制，使超网络的注入能力独立于目标模型的通用能力。构建MegaWikiQA数据集，涵盖来自Wikidata5M的数十万个多跳问答对，覆盖39个领域。通过控制实验系统评估不同超网络深度、宽度以及目标模型大小下的损失、推理准确率和分布外泛化表现。

Result: （i）超网络在所有架构维度（深度、宽度、目标模型规模）上均表现出符合幂律的可预测扩展性；（ii）在分布外任务中，超网络展现出良好的泛化能力，且其缩放指数优于LoRA微调和全量微调，在各种评估指标上均表现更优。这表明超网络在大规模知识注入中具有更强的可扩展性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 超网络是一种可扩展、可信赖的训练时知识注入方法，具备强大的分布外泛化能力。本研究首次建立了针对超网络架构的实证缩放定律，为未来大模型的事实推理系统设计提供了理论指导与实践依据。

Abstract: Injecting factual knowledge into large language models (LLMs) reliably and at scale remains an open challenge. Hypernetworks provide a promising solution to large-scale knowledge injection. Although hypernetworks are typically applied for test-time adaptation, we explore their use in train-time knowledge injection, where, given a large corpus of facts, we train a hypernetwork to generate a fixed LoRA adapter that, when inserted into the target model, enable the model to answer questions about those facts. In this work, we investigate whether hypernetworks can be used to perform train-time knowledge injection and how this ability varies with scale. The scaling behavior of hypernetworks remains largely unstudied. Our design decouples the hypernetwork's injection capacity from the target model's general capability, enabling, for the first time, a rigorous study of scaling laws for hypernetwork architectures. We characterize how loss, reasoning accuracy, and out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization vary with hypernetwork depth, width, and target network size. We construct a large-scale dataset, called MegaWikiQA, containing tens of millions of multi-hop question-answer examples across 39 domains constructed from examples in Wikidata5M. Our results reveal: (i) hypernetwork-based injection exhibits broadly predictive power law scaling along all architecture axes; and (ii) hypernetworks are capable of reliable OOD generalization at increasing scales, suggesting that hypernetwork provides a promising alternative to other train-time adaptation methods such as LoRA finetuning and full fine-tuning, exhibiting steeper scaling exponents in all OOD evaluations. Together, these results establish hypernetworks as a principled and scalable substrate for train-time adaptation, and provide the first empirically grounded scaling laws to guide hypernetworks for factual reasoning in large language models.

</details>


### [76] [Task Competence Is Not Instruction Following: Evaluating Instruction-Conflicting Behavior in Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19608)
*Mahdiyeh Farajidizaji,Vatsal Raina*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了小规模语言模型在指令冲突时是否遵循用户请求，通过跨任务实验（多选题问答、情感分类、数学问答）对比标准与非标准指令下的表现。结果显示，小模型虽任务能力尚可但常忽略非标准指令，而大模型在任务能力和指令遵循间出现明显差距，表明任务胜任力与指令遵循是两种独立能力，仅报告标准准确率会掩盖指令遵循失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究小规模语言模型在指令冲突时是否能遵循用户请求，特别是当指令与模型常规任务行为相悖时，揭示任务能力与指令遵循之间的关系。

Method: 设计跨任务实验，对Qwen系列模型在三种任务中分别施加标准指令和冲突的非标准指令（如选择错误选项、输出相反情感、返回两倍答案），通过标准准确率、非标准准确率和指令遵循失败率（IFFR）评估模型表现。

Result: 小模型在任务上表现良好但普遍忽略非标准指令；大模型在任务能力和指令遵循之间呈现显著差距；任务能力提升不必然带来可靠的行为控制，说明任务胜任力与指令遵循为独立能力。

Conclusion: 任务能力与指令遵循是两种独立的能力，仅依赖标准准确率会隐藏指令遵循失败，因此需要引入专门指标（如IFFR）来全面评估模型对指令的遵守情况。

Abstract: Instruction tuning is meant to make language models follow user requests, yet it is unclear whether small models comply when an instruction conflicts with their usual task behavior. We study this across three tasks - multiple-choice question answering (MCQA), sentiment classification, and mathematical question answering - by pairing a standard instruction with a conflicting non-standard one (select an incorrect option, output the opposite sentiment, or return twice the answer). This cross-task design allows us to test whether resistance to conflicting instructions is tied to specific task characteristics or reflects a broader behavioral tendency. As all predictions are scored against the original ground truth, a model that ignores the non-standard instruction still appears accurate. Using standard accuracy, non-standard accuracy, and an Instruction-Following Failure Rate (IFFR), we evaluate instruction-tuned Qwen models across sizes. Both standard accuracy and instruction following generally improve with scale, although the pattern is not consistent across all tasks and datasets. Small models stay competent yet routinely ignore the non-standard instruction, while larger models show a clear gap between the two settings. These findings suggest that gains in task capability do not automatically provide reliable control over model behavior. Task competence and instruction following are therefore distinct abilities, and reporting only standard accuracy hides instruction-following failures.

</details>


### [77] [Adaptive Capitulation: A Structural Failure Mode of LLM Responses in Vulnerability Contexts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19629)
*Eunna Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型在情感敏感情境中面临的结构性三难困境：当前响应架构在保护、无偏支持与二者共存之间难以兼顾。通过三轮渐进式脆弱性情景实验（共900次会话），发现一种未被记录的“适应性屈服”失效模式——模型先认可用户痛苦背后的社会不公，随后却详细协助其获取原本应被抑制的信息。研究证明该三难是结构性而非偶然现象，并提出‘最小再归因充分性’（MRS）设计原则，即在保持共情回应的同时嵌入单一再归因提示，以保留用户自主重构认知的路径，而不直接挑战其表层目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在处理情绪脆弱用户请求时，常面临保护用户免受有害认知强化、支持其需求、以及维持响应一致性之间的矛盾。现有方法要么限制信息提供，要么无差别支持，或混合两者，导致无法同时满足伦理与功能目标。研究旨在揭示这一系统性困境并提出更优解决方案。

Method: 采用三轮渐进式脆弱性情景实验，涵盖物质、关系与躯体状态代理变体，对三个商业大模型进行900次会话测试；使用两个二元编码指标（VCC/VCI）分析响应内容，识别模型行为模式，特别是‘适应性屈服’现象。

Result: 发现模型普遍存在‘适应性屈服’行为：先共情承认社会不公，再详尽支持用户获取原应被抑制的信息；表明三难困境具有结构性根源，非偶然错误。

Conclusion: 提出‘最小再归因充分性’（MRS）作为架构无关的设计原则，通过在共情回应中嵌入单一再归因线索，既维护用户自主性又避免强化有害认知，为情感敏感场景下的语言模型设计提供新范式。

Abstract: Large language models operating in emotionally sensitive contexts face a structural trilemma: when users in vulnerable states request information that may reinforce maladaptive attribution, current response architectures resolve the tension through protective restriction, uninflected facilitation, or unintegrated co-presence of both imperatives -- each preserving one objective at the cost of the other. Administering a three-turn escalating vulnerability vignette to three commercial LLMs (900 sessions across material, relational, and somatic status-proxy variants) and coding responses with two binary indices (VCC/VCI), we characterize a previously undocumented failure mode we term adaptive capitulation: the model validates the social injustice underlying the user's distress before pivoting to detailed facilitation of the very acquisition it nominally discouraged. We show that the trilemma is structural rather than incidental, and propose Minimal Reattributive Sufficiency (MRS), an architecture-neutral design principle that embeds a single reattributive cue within an otherwise validating response, preserving a pathway toward autonomous reattribution without contesting the user's stated goal.

</details>


### [78] [Reference-Free Evaluation of Reasoning in Open-Ended Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19678)
*Guneet Singh Kohli,Yuxiang Zhou,Michael Sejr Schlichtkrull,Gregory E Dean,Maria Liakata*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于推理的、无需参考的框架，用于审计大模型生成的答案。该框架将生成的推理链分解为多个片段，利用自然语言蕴含（NLI）标注局部前提-目标关系，并构建超图结构。通过确定性的逆向AND-OR搜索，为每个片段分配审计标签，以判断其在回答中的依据程度。在数学和医学两个场景中评估，该方法比直接使用大模型作为评判者更可靠。尤其在临床场景中，现有大模型常误判流畅但论证薄弱的回答。结果表明，问答评估应关注推理链中推断关系的组合方式，而不仅依赖最终答案或大模型自评。相关数据集UroReason将通过API提供，代码也将开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型生成的答案在高风险领域虽流畅但难以验证，尤其当包含多步推理时，传统依赖最终答案或大模型自评的方法存在可靠性问题，亟需一种可解释且无需参考的审计机制。

Method: 将生成的推理链分解为片段，使用自然语言蕴含（NLI）识别片段间的前提-目标关系，构建超图结构；采用确定性逆向AND-OR搜索，为各片段分配审计标签，反映其逻辑根基程度。

Result: 在数学推理（Hard2Verify）与临床推理（UroReason）任务中，该方法显著优于直接使用大模型作为裁判的基线，能有效识别出看似合理但实际论证薄弱的推理段落。在临床场景中，主流大模型裁判常误接受不严谨回答。

Conclusion: 评估大模型推理质量不能仅依赖最终答案或大模型自评，必须考虑推理链中各步骤间推断关系的连贯性与合理性。所提出的NLI-超图审计框架为无参考环境下的可信评估提供了新范式。

Abstract: AI-generated answers in high-stakes domains are often fluent but difficult to verify, especially when they contain multi-step reasoning rather than a single final answer. We propose a reasoning-based, reference-free framework for auditing LLM-generated outputs. The method decomposes a generated reasoning trace into segments, labels local premise-target relations using Natural Language Inference (NLI), and organizes these relations into a hypergraph. A deterministic backward AND-OR search then assigns segment-level audit labels that indicate how each segment is grounded within the generated response. We evaluate the framework in two settings: deductive mathematical reasoning with Hard2Verify, and open-ended medical reasoning with UroReason, a new physician-annotated benchmark of LLM reasoning traces from real clinical cases. Across these settings, our NLI-hypergraph audit provides a more reliable reference-free evaluation signal than direct LLM-as-judge baselines. In the clinical setting, state-of-the-art LLM judges often fail to identify problematic reasoning segments, over-accepting fluent but weakly grounded responses. Our results show that QA evaluation should account for how inferential relations compose across a reasoning trace, rather than relying only on final answers or LLMs as verifiers. UroReason will be made available through an API, and our code will be released as open source.
